<script>
(function sortbarDropdown() {
var sortbarContainer;
var sortbarOptionsContainer;
var sortbarOptions;
var sortByStarsButton;
var dropdownContainer;
var dropdownOptionsContainer;
var dropdownButton;
var movedOptions;
var dropdownIsNeeded;
function setup() {
sortbarContainer = document.getElementById('sort_by');
if (!!sortbarContainer) {
sortbarOptionsContainer = sortbarContainer.querySelector('ul');
sortbarOptions = [].slice.call(sortbarOptionsContainer.querySelectorAll('.sort_category'));
sortByStarsButton = sortbarOptionsContainer.querySelector('.sort_class > .sort_option');
dropdownContainer = document.getElementById('sortbar_dropdown_container');
dropdownOptionsContainer = document.getElementById('sortbar_dropdown_options');
dropdownButton = document.getElementById('sortbar_dropdown_button');
movedOptions = [];
dropdownIsNeeded = false;
prepare();
moveSelectedAndGeniusUp();
buildDropdown();
moveSelectedAndGeniusBeforeDropdown();
finalize();
}
}
function prepare() {
sortbarContainer.style.visibility = 'hidden';
dropdownContainer.style.display = 'none';
sortbarContainer.style.width = '680px';
}
function finalize() {
dropdownContainer.style.display = dropdownIsNeeded ? '' : 'none';
sortbarContainer.style.width = '';
sortbarContainer.style.visibility = 'visible';
if (dropdownIsNeeded) {
sortbarContainer.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
if (dropdownButton.contains(event.target)) {
dropdownOptionsContainer.classList.toggle('is-visible');
} else if (!dropdownOptionsContainer.contains(event.target)) {
dropdownOptionsContainer.classList.remove('is-visible');
} else if (sortByStarsButton && !sortByStarsButton.contains(event.target)) {
dropdownOptionsContainer.classList.remove('is-visible');
}
});
document.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
if (!!sortbarContainer && !sortbarContainer.contains(event.target)) {
dropdownOptionsContainer.classList.remove('is-visible');
}
});
} else {
dropdownContainer.parentNode.removeChild(dropdownContainer);
}
}
function moveSelectedAndGeniusUp() {
for(var i = sortbarOptions.length; i--;) {
if (!!sortbarOptions[i].offsetTop) {
if (sortbarOptions[i].classList.contains('selected') || sortbarOptions[i].classList.contains('sort_genius')) {
movedOptions.push(sortbarOptions[i]);
sortbarOptionsContainer.insertBefore(sortbarOptions[i], sortbarOptionsContainer.firstChild);
}
} else {
break;
}
}
if (!!movedOptions.length) {
for(var i = movedOptions.length; i--;) {
sortbarOptions.sort(function(a, b){
return a === movedOptions[i] ? -1 : b === movedOptions[i] ? 1 : 0;
});
}
}
}
function moveSelectedAndGeniusBeforeDropdown() {
if (!!movedOptions.length) {
for(var i = movedOptions.length; i--;) {
sortbarOptionsContainer.insertBefore(movedOptions[i], dropdownContainer);
}
}
}
function buildDropdown() {
var dropdownOptions = [];
for(var i = sortbarOptions.length; i--;) {
if (!!sortbarOptions[i].offsetTop) {
dropdownIsNeeded = true;
dropdownOptions.push(sortbarOptions[i]);
} else {
break;
}
}
if (dropdownIsNeeded) {
for(var i = dropdownOptions.length; i--;) {
dropdownOptionsContainer.appendChild(dropdownOptions[i]);
}
}
}
function ajaxSetup() {
function callback() {
if (!!B && !!B.require) {
var events = B.require('searchresults/events');
events.on(events.UI_BLOCK_UPDATED, function (e) {
if (e.id === 'sort_bar') {
setup();
}
});
}
}
if (document.attachEvent ? document.readyState === "complete" : document.readyState !== "loading") {
callback();
} else {
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', callback);
}
}
setup();
ajaxSetup();
}());
</script>

function blockdisplay(i) {
var body = $( document.body );
if (document.getElementById("blockdisplay" + i)) {
for (var j = 1; j <= 4; j++) {
if (document.getElementById('blockdisplay' + j)) {
document.getElementById('blockdisplay' + j).style.display = (j === i) ? 'block' : 'none';
}
}
body.trigger((i == 4) ? 'ReviewsTab_onOpen' : 'ReviewsTab_onClose')
.trigger( 'RT:reset' );
( booking.eventEmitter || $( window ) )
.trigger( 'BLOCKDISPLAY' + i + '.OPEN' );
if (i === 1 && typeof bMovableBookNowButton != "undefined") {
bMovableBookNowButton.init();
}
if (i == 4) {
$(".toggle_overview").show();
$(".toggle_review").hide();
} else {
$(".toggle_review").show();
$(".toggle_overview").hide();
}
}
